                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>

    <form n="infl">       
                     <orth orig="Bu" lang="ar">اَكُلَ</orth>
                  </form>,] inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">أَكْلٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">مَأْكَلٌ</foreign>, [<hi rend="ital">He ate it,</hi>] (S, K,) namely, food. (S.) Er-Rummánee says that <foreign lang="ar">أَكْلٌ</foreign> properly signifies The <hi rend="ital">swallowing</hi> food <hi rend="ital">after chewing</hi> it; so that the swallowing of pebbles is not properly thus termed: (Msb:) or, accord. to Ibn-El-Kemál, the <hi rend="ital">conveying,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">transmitting, to the belly</hi> what may be chewed, <hi rend="ital">whether</hi> [<hi rend="ital">the thing be</hi>] <hi rend="ital">chewed or not;</hi> so that it does not apply to milk, nor to <foreign lang="ar">سَوِيق</foreign>: and as to the saying of the poet, <quote>
                     <L>
                        <foreign lang="ar">مِنَ الآكِلِينَ المَآءَ ظُلْمًا فَمَا أَرَى</foreign>
                     </L> 
                     <L>
                        <foreign lang="ar">يَنَالُونَ خَيْرًا بَعْدَ أَكْلِهِمُ المَآءَ</foreign>
                     </L> 
                  </quote> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  [<hi rend="ital">Of the eaters of</hi> what they purchase with the price of <hi rend="ital">water, wrongfully, I do not see</hi> any <hi rend="ital">attain good after their eating of</hi> what they have purchased with the price of <hi rend="ital">the water,</hi>] he means a people who used to sell water and purchase with the price thereof what they would eat: (TA:) [for you say, <foreign lang="ar">أَكَلَ كَذَا</foreign> as meaning <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">He ate the price of such a thing:</hi> see another ex. voce <foreign lang="ar">إِكَافٌ</foreign>; and another voce <foreign lang="ar">ثَدْىٌ</foreign>.]          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  The saying, in the Kur [v. 70], <foreign lang="ar">لَأَكَلُوا مِنْ فَوْقِهِمْ وَمِنْ تَحْتِ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">أَرْجُلِهِمْ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">They should eat</hi> things <hi rend="ital">above them and</hi> things <hi rend="ital">beneath their feet</hi>] means, their means of subsistence should be made ample; (Bd, TA;) by the pouring of the blessings of the heaven and the earth upon them; or by the abundance of the fruit of the trees, and the produce of the grains sown; or by their being blessed with gardens of ripe fruits, so that they should gather them from the upper part of each tree, and pick up what should have fallen upon the ground. (Bd.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">اِنْقَطَعَ أَكْلُهُ</foreign> [lit. <hi rend="ital">His eating became cut off,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">stopped,</hi>] means <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">he died;</hi> [see also <foreign lang="ar">أُكُلٌ</foreign>;] and so <foreign lang="ar">اِسْتَوْفَى أَكْلَهُ</foreign> [lit. <hi rend="ital">he completed his eating</hi>]. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">أَكَلَ رَؤْقَهُ</foreign> [lit. <hi rend="ital">He ate his life,</hi>] means <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">he became extremely aged, and his teeth fell out, one after another.</hi> (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="5">-b5-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">هُوَ يَأْكُلُ النَّاسَ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">يَأْكُلُ لُحُومَ النَّاسِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He eats men,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">eats the flesh of men,</hi>] means <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">he defames men;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">does so in their absence:</hi> (TA:) and the action thus signified may be [<hi rend="ital">with words, or by making signs</hi>] <hi rend="ital">with the side of the mouth,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">with the eye,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">with the head.</hi> (TA in art. <foreign lang="ar">همز</foreign>.) It is said in the Kur [xlix. 12], <foreign lang="ar">أَيُحِبُّ أَحَدُكُمْ أَنْ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">يَأْكلَ لَحْمَ أَخِيهِ مَيْتًا</foreign> [lit. <hi rend="ital">Would any one of you like to eat the flesh of his brother when dead?</hi>]; defamation, or defamation of the absent, being meant thereby. (S, * Ibn-' Arafeh, Bd, Jel.)          <sense type="b" n="6">-b6-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">أَكَلَ غَنَمِى وَ شَرِبَهَا</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">He ate</hi> the flesh of <hi rend="ital">my sheep, and drank</hi> the milk of <hi rend="ital">them,</hi> means, like <foreign lang="ar">أَكَلَ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">مَالِى</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">he ate, fed upon, devoured,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">consumed, my wealth,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">property:</hi> see 2]. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="7">-b7-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">أَكَلَتِ النَّارُ الحَطَبَ</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">The fire devoured,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">consumed, the firewood.</hi> (S, Mgh.)          <sense type="b" n="8">-b8-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">أَكَلَتْ أَظْفَارَهُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">الحِجَارَةُ</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">The stones wore away his nails</hi>]. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="9">-b9-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">الوَاوُ فِى مَرْئىٍّ أَكَلَتْهَا اليَآءُ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  [<hi rend="ital">The</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">و</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">in</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">مَرْئِىّ</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">the</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">ى</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">has swallowed it up</hi>]; because it is originally <foreign lang="ar">مَرْؤُوىٌ</foreign>: a phrase occurring in the 'Eyn. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="10">-b10-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">أَكَلَ عُمُرَهُ</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">He consumed his life.</hi> (Mgh.)          <sense type="b" n="11">-b11-</sense>  It is said in a trad., (TA,) <foreign lang="ar">أُمِرْتُ بِقَرْيَةٍ تَأْكُلُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">القُرَى</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">I have been commanded to have given unto me a town which shall devour the</hi> other <hi rend="ital">towns</hi>]; (K, TA;) said to be Yethrib [afterwards called El-Medeeneh]; (TA;) i. e., the people of which shall conquer the [other] towns and make spoil of their possessions: or it denotes the superior excellence of that town; and is like the saying, <foreign lang="ar">هٰذَا حَدِيثٌ يَأْكُلُ الأَحَادِيثَ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">This is a tradition which does away with,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">overrules, the</hi> other <hi rend="ital">traditions</hi>]. (Sgh. K, TA.)          <sense type="b" n="12">-b12-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">أَكْلُ السِّكِّينِ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">اللَّحْمَ</foreign> means <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">The knife's cutting the flesh.</hi> (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="13">-b13-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">أَكَلَنِي رَأْسِى</foreign>, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">إِكْلَةٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">أُكَالٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">أَكَالٌ</foreign>, <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">My head itched.</hi> (K, TA.) An Arab was heard to say, [as is often said in the present day,] <foreign lang="ar">جِلْدِى يَأْكُلُنِى</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">My skin itches.</hi> (TA.)       <sense type="A" n="2">-A2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">أَكِلَ</foreign>, aor.      
    <form n="infl">       
                     <orth orig="Ba" lang="ar">اَكَلَ</orth>
                  </form>, (K,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">أَكَلٌ</foreign>, (TA,) <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">It</hi> (a limb, or member, [and a sore,] and a piece of stick, or wood,) <hi rend="ital">became corroded</hi> or <hi rend="ital">cankered,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">decayed, by the mutual eating away of its several parts;</hi> as also
